   166‚Üí// Enhanced GlassDropdown component with liquid glass styling
   167‚Üíexport function GlassDropdown({
   168‚Üí  trigger,
   169‚Üí  content,
   170‚Üí  children,
   171‚Üí}: {
   172‚Üí  trigger?: React.ReactNode;
   173‚Üí  content?: React.ReactNode;
   174‚Üí  children?: React.ReactNode;
   175‚Üí}) {
   176‚Üí  return (
   177‚Üí    <div className='relative inline-block'>
   178‚Üí      <div
   179‚Üí        className='apple-liquid-glass p-4 rounded-xl glass-magnetic animate-spring-entrance relative overflow-hidden'
   180‚Üí        style={{
   181‚Üí          backdropFilter: 'blur(16px) saturate(180%)',
   182‚Üí          WebkitBackdropFilter: 'blur(16px) saturate(180%)',
   183‚Üí          background: 'rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.15)',
   184‚Üí          border: '1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.2)',
   185‚Üí          boxShadow: `
   186‚Üí            0 8px 32px rgba(31, 38, 135, 0.2),
   187‚Üí            0 0 0 1px rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1),
   188‚Üí            inset 0 1px 0 rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.3)
   189‚Üí          `,
   190‚Üí        }}
   191‚Üí      >
   192‚Üí        <p className='text-white/90 text-sm mb-3 font-medium'>
   193‚Üí          <span className='text-blue-200'>‚ú® GlassDropdown Demo</span> -
   194‚Üí          Interactive showcase component
   195‚Üí        </p>
   196‚Üí        {trigger && (
   197‚Üí          <div className='mb-2'>
   198‚Üí            <span className='text-white/70 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider'>
   199‚Üí              Trigger:
   200‚Üí            </span>
   201‚Üí            <div className='mt-1'>{trigger}</div>
   202‚Üí          </div>
   203‚Üí        )}
   204‚Üí        {content && (
   205‚Üí          <div className='mt-3'>
   206‚Üí            <span className='text-white/70 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider'>
   207‚Üí              Content:
   208‚Üí            </span>
   209‚Üí            <div className='mt-1'>{content}</div>
   210‚Üí          </div>
   211‚Üí        )}
   212‚Üí        {children}
   213‚Üí        <div
   214‚Üí          className='absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-br from-white/10 via-transparent to-transparent pointer-events-none'
   215‚Üí          style={{
   216‚Üí            background:
   217‚Üí              'radial-gradient(circle at 50% 0%, rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.2) 0%, transparent 60%)',
   218‚Üí          }}
   219‚Üí        />
   220‚Üí      </div>
   221‚Üí    </div>
   222‚Üí  );
   223‚Üí}
   224‚Üí
   225‚Üí// Enhanced GlassTab component with liquid glass styling
   226‚Üíexport function GlassTab({
   227‚Üí  children,
   228‚Üí  ...props
   229‚Üí}: React.ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement>) {
   230‚Üí  return (
   231‚Üí    <button

   238‚Üí        boxShadow: `
   239‚Üí          0 4px 16px rgba(31, 38, 135, 0.15),
   240‚Üí          0 0 0 1px rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1),
   241‚Üí          inset 0 1px 0 rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.3)
   242‚Üí        `,
   243‚Üí      }}
   244‚Üí      {...props}
   245‚Üí    >
   246‚Üí      <span className='relative z-10 text-white/90 font-medium'>
   247‚Üí        {children}
   248‚Üí      </span>
   249‚Üí      <div
   250‚Üí        className='absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-transparent via-white/10 to-transparent opacity-0 hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-300'
   251‚Üí        style={{
   252‚Üí          background:
   253‚Üí            'linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1) 0%, rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.05) 50%, rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1) 100%)',
   254‚Üí        }}
   255‚Üí      />
   256‚Üí    </button>
   257‚Üí  );
   258‚Üí}
   259‚Üí
   260‚Üíexport function GlassTabs({
   261‚Üí  children,
   262‚Üí  ...props
   263‚Üí}: React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>) {
   264‚Üí  return (
   265‚Üí    <div
   266‚Üí      className='flex space-x-1 p-1 apple-liquid-glass rounded-xl glass-magnetic animate-spring-entrance relative overflow-hidden'
   267‚Üí      style={{
   268‚Üí        backdropFilter: 'blur(16px) saturate(180%)',
   269‚Üí        WebkitBackdropFilter: 'blur(16px) saturate(180%)',
   270‚Üí        background: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.08)',
   271‚Üí        border: '1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.15)',
   272‚Üí        boxShadow: `
   273‚Üí          0 6px 24px rgba(31, 38, 135, 0.15),
   274‚Üí          0 0 0 1px rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1),
   275‚Üí          inset 0 1px 0 rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.2)
   276‚Üí        `,
   277‚Üí      }}
   278‚Üí      {...props}
   279‚Üí    >
   280‚Üí      {children}
   281‚Üí      <div
   282‚Üí        className='absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-white/5 via-transparent to-white/5 pointer-events-none'
   283‚Üí        style={{
   284‚Üí          background:
   285‚Üí            'radial-gradient(ellipse at center, rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.05) 0%, transparent 70%)',
   286‚Üí        }}
   287‚Üí      />
   288‚Üí    </div>
   289‚Üí  );
   290‚Üí}
   291‚Üí
   292‚Üíinterface ClientWrapperProps {
   293‚Üí  children: ReactNode;
   294‚Üí}
   295‚Üí
   296‚Üíexport function ClientWrapper({ children }: ClientWrapperProps) {
   297‚Üí  const [mounted, setMounted] = useState(false);
   298‚Üí
   299‚Üí  useEffect(() => {
   300‚Üí    setMounted(true);
   301‚Üí  }, []);
   302‚Üí
   303‚Üí  if (!mounted) {
   304‚Üí    return <div style={{ display: 'contents' }}>{children}</div>;
   305‚Üí  }
   306‚Üí
   307‚Üí  return <LiquidGlassProvider>{children}</LiquidGlassProvider>;
   308‚Üí}
   309‚Üí
   310‚Üíexport default ClientWrapper;
   311‚Üí

Result:

```
1‚Üí# Glass Button
     2‚Üí
     3‚ÜíA premium glass-effect button component with advanced visual effects, multiple variants, loading states, and full accessibility support.
     4‚Üí
     5‚Üí## Overview
     6‚Üí
     7‚ÜíThe Glass Button is an interactive element that enables users to initiate actions, make choices, or navigate through interfaces. Built with sophisticated glassmorphism effects, backdrop blur, magnetic hover interactions, and haptic feedback support, it provides an elegant user experience while maintaining full accessibility compliance.
     8‚Üí
     9‚Üí## Features
    10‚Üí
    11‚Üí- **Multiple Variants**: 5 visual styles (primary, secondary, tertiary, ghost, destructive)
    12‚Üí- **5 Size Options**: xs, sm, md, lg, xl following 4pt grid system
    13‚Üí- **Loading States**: Built-in spinner with smooth transitions
    14‚Üí- **Icon Support**: Left and right icons with proper spacing
    15‚Üí- **Glass Morphism**: Advanced backdrop blur and transparency effects
    16‚Üí- **Magnetic Hover**: Subtle magnetic attraction interactions
    17‚Üí- **Haptic Feedback**: Native haptic response on supported devices
    18‚Üí- **Accessibility**: Full VoiceOver, Voice Control, and keyboard support
    19‚Üí
    20‚Üí## Anatomy
    21‚Üí
    22‚ÜíThe Glass Button consists of:
    23‚Üí
    24‚Üí- **Container**: Glass surface with backdrop blur and border
    25‚Üí- **Label**: Text content with Apple HIG typography
    26‚Üí- **Icons** (optional): Leading or trailing visual elements
    27‚Üí- **Loading Spinner** (optional): Animated loading indicator
    28‚Üí- **Focus Ring**: Blue accessibility indicator
    29‚Üí- **Magnetic Field**: Invisible hover interaction zone
    30‚Üí
    31‚Üí## API Reference
    32‚Üí
    33‚Üí### Props
    34‚Üí
    35‚ÜíBased on the actual Liquidify component API:
    36‚Üí
    37‚Üí| Prop                    | Type                                                                 | Default     | Description                                    |
    38‚Üí| ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------- | ----------- | ---------------------------------------------- |
    39‚Üí| `variant`               | `'primary' \| 'secondary' \| 'tertiary' \| 'ghost' \| 'destructive'` | `'primary'` | Visual style and prominence                    |
    40‚Üí| `size`                  | `'xs' \| 'sm' \| 'md' \| 'lg' \| 'xl'`                               | `'md'`      | Button size following 4pt grid                 |
    41‚Üí| `asChild`               | `boolean`                                                            | `false`     | Render as child component (Slot pattern)       |
    42‚Üí| `leftIcon`              | `ReactNode`                                                          | `undefined` | Icon displayed on the left side                |
    43‚Üí| `rightIcon`             | `ReactNode`                                                          | `undefined` | Icon displayed on the right side               |
    44‚Üí| `loading`               | `boolean`                                                            | `false`     | Shows loading spinner and disables interaction |
    45‚Üí| `disabled`              | `boolean`                                                            | `false`     | Disables button interaction                    |
    46‚Üí| `className`             | `string`                                                             | `undefined` | Additional CSS classes                         |
    47‚Üí| `children`              | `ReactNode`                                                          | -           | Button content                                 |
    48‚Üí| ...HTMLButtonAttributes | -                                                                    | -           | All standard button HTML attributes            |
    49‚Üí
    50‚Üí### Size Specifications
    51‚Üí
    52‚ÜíFrom the component tokens:
    53‚Üí
    54‚Üí- **xs**: 28px height, 8px/10px padding
    55‚Üí- **sm**: 32px height, 10px/12px padding
    56‚Üí- **md**: 40px height, 12px/16px padding (default)
    57‚Üí- **lg**: 44px height, 14px/20px padding
    58‚Üí- **xl**: 52px height, 16px/24px padding
    59‚Üí
    60‚Üí## Code Examples
    61‚Üí
    62‚Üí### Basic Usage
    63‚Üí
    64‚Üí\```tsx
    65‚Üíimport { GlassButton } from 'liquidify';
    66‚Üí
    67‚Üíexport default function BasicExample() {
    68‚Üí  return (
    69‚Üí    <GlassButton variant='primary' size='md'>
    70‚Üí      Get Started
    71‚Üí    </GlassButton>
    72‚Üí  );

   103‚Üí### Loading State
   104‚Üí
   105‚Üí\```tsx
   106‚Üíimport { GlassButton } from 'liquidify';
   107‚Üíimport { useState } from 'react';
   108‚Üí
   109‚Üíexport default function LoadingExample() {
   110‚Üí  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
   111‚Üí
   112‚Üí  const handleSubmit = async () => {
   113‚Üí    setLoading(true);
   114‚Üí    try {
   115‚Üí      // Simulate API call
   116‚Üí      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2000));
   117‚Üí      console.log('Form submitted!');
   118‚Üí    } finally {
   119‚Üí      setLoading(false);
   120‚Üí    }
   121‚Üí  };
   122‚Üí
   123‚Üí  return (
   124‚Üí    <GlassButton
   125‚Üí      variant='primary'
   126‚Üí      loading={loading}
   127‚Üí      onClick={handleSubmit}
   128‚Üí      disabled={loading}
   129‚Üí    >
   130‚Üí      {loading ? 'Submitting...' : 'Submit Form'}
   131‚Üí    </GlassButton>
   132‚Üí  );
   133‚Üí}
   134‚Üí\```

   158‚Üí### All Sizes
   159‚Üí
   160‚Üí\```tsx
   161‚Üíimport { GlassButton } from 'liquidify';
   162‚Üí
   163‚Üíexport default function SizesExample() {
   164‚Üí  return (
   165‚Üí    <div className='flex items-end gap-4'>
   166‚Üí      <GlassButton size='xs'>Extra Small</GlassButton>
   167‚Üí      <GlassButton size='sm'>Small</GlassButton>
   168‚Üí      <GlassButton size='md'>Medium</GlassButton>
   169‚Üí      <GlassButton size='lg'>Large</GlassButton>
   170‚Üí      <GlassButton size='xl'>Extra Large</GlassButton>
   171‚Üí    </div>
   172‚Üí  );
   173‚Üí}
   174‚Üí\```
   175‚Üí
   176‚Üí### As Child Pattern
   177‚Üí
   178‚Üí\```tsx
   179‚Üíimport { GlassButton } from 'liquidify';
   180‚Üíimport Link from 'next/link';
   181‚Üí
   182‚Üíexport default function AsChildExample() {
   183‚Üí  return (
   184‚Üí    <GlassButton asChild>
   185‚Üí      <Link href='/docs' className='inline-flex items-center'>
   186‚Üí        View Documentation
   187‚Üí      </Link>
   188‚Üí    </GlassButton>
   189‚Üí  );
   190‚Üí}
   191‚Üí\```
   192‚Üí
   193‚Üí## Dynamic Configuration
   194‚Üí
   195‚ÜíYou can combine different props to create various button styles:
   196‚Üí
   197‚Üí\```tsx
   198‚Üíimport { GlassButton } from 'liquidify';
   199‚Üíimport { useState } from 'react';
   200‚Üí
   201‚Üífunction ConfigurableButton() {
   202‚Üí  const [variant, setVariant] = useState('primary');
   203‚Üí  const [size, setSize] = useState('md');
   204‚Üí  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
   205‚Üí
   206‚Üí  return (
   207‚Üí    <div className='space-y-4'>
   208‚Üí      <div className='flex gap-4'>
   209‚Üí        <select value={variant} onChange={e => setVariant(e.target.value)}>
   210‚Üí          <option value='primary'>Primary</option>
   211‚Üí          <option value='secondary'>Secondary</option>
   212‚Üí          <option value='tertiary'>Tertiary</option>
   213‚Üí          <option value='ghost'>Ghost</option>
   214‚Üí          <option value='destructive'>Destructive</option>
   215‚Üí        </select>
   216‚Üí
   217‚Üí        <select value={size} onChange={e => setSize(e.target.value)}>
   218‚Üí          <option value='xs'>XS</option>
   219‚Üí          <option value='sm'>SM</option>
   220‚Üí          <option value='md'>MD</option>
   221‚Üí          <option value='lg'>LG</option>
   222‚Üí          <option value='xl'>XL</option>
   223‚Üí        </select>
   224‚Üí
   225‚Üí        <label>
   226‚Üí          <input
   227‚Üí            type='checkbox'
   228‚Üí            checked={loading}
   229‚Üí            onChange={e => setLoading(e.target.checked)}
   230‚Üí          />
   231‚Üí          Loading
   232‚Üí        </label>
   233‚Üí      </div>
   234‚Üí
   235‚Üí      <GlassButton variant={variant} size={size} loading={loading}>
   236‚Üí        Dynamic Button
   237‚Üí      </GlassButton>
   238‚Üí    </div>
   239‚Üí  );
   240‚Üí}
   241‚Üí\```
   242‚Üí
   243‚Üí## Accessibility
   244‚Üí
   245‚Üí### VoiceOver Support
   246‚Üí
   247‚Üí- Proper semantic button role
   248‚Üí- Clear, descriptive labels
   249‚Üí- State announcements for loading/disabled states
   250‚Üí
   251‚Üí### Voice Control
   252‚Üí
   253‚Üí- Responds to "Tap [button text]" commands
   254‚Üí- Supports number-based navigation
   255‚Üí- Handles icon-only buttons with accessibility labels
   256‚Üí
   257‚Üí### Keyboard Navigation
   258‚Üí
   259‚Üí- **Tab**: Focus button
   260‚Üí- **Space/Enter**: Activate button
   261‚Üí- **Escape**: Remove focus (when appropriate)
   262‚Üí
   263‚Üí### High Contrast Mode
   264‚Üí
   265‚Üí- Maintains proper contrast ratios
   266‚Üí- Enhanced borders and focus indicators
   267‚Üí- Respects system contrast preferences
   268‚Üí
   269‚Üí### Reduced Motion
   270‚Üí
   271‚Üí- Respects `prefers-reduced-motion`
   272‚Üí- Provides alternative feedback for animations
   273‚Üí- Maintains functionality without motion
   274‚Üí
   275‚Üí## Design Tokens
   276‚Üí
   277‚ÜíThe component uses Liquidify's design token system:
   278‚Üí
   279‚Üí### Colors
   280‚Üí
   281‚Üí\```css
   282‚Üí/* Primary variant uses system blue */
   283‚Üí--glass-primary-bg: rgba(0, 122, 255, 0.15);
   284‚Üí--glass-primary-border: rgba(0, 122, 255, 0.3);
   285‚Üí--glass-primary-text: #007aff;
   286‚Üí
   287‚Üí/* Secondary uses subtle glass */
   288‚Üí--glass-secondary-bg: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1);
   289‚Üí--glass-secondary-border: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.2);
   290‚Üí\```
   291‚Üí
   292‚Üí### Typography
   293‚Üí
   294‚ÜíUses system font stack with appropriate weights:
   295‚Üí
   296‚Üí\```css
   297‚Üífont-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'SF Pro Display', sans-serif;
   298‚Üí\```
   299‚Üí
   300‚Üí### Spacing & Sizing
   301‚Üí
   302‚ÜíFollows 4pt grid system with precise touch targets:
   303‚Üí
   304‚Üí\```css
   305‚Üí/* Medium size (default) */
   306‚Üíheight: 40px;
   307‚Üípadding: 12px 16px;
   308‚Üímin-width: 44px; /* Touch target compliance */
   309‚Üí\```
   310‚Üí
   311‚Üí### Glass Effects
   312‚Üí
   313‚Üí\```css
   314‚Üíbackdrop-filter: blur(20px) saturate(180%);
   315‚Üí-webkit-backdrop-filter: blur(20px) saturate(180%);
   316‚Üíbackground: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.12);
   317‚Üíborder: 1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.18);
   318‚Üí\```
   319‚Üí

    70‚Üí
    71‚Üí// Enhanced SSR-safe glass effect component for MDX components
    72‚Üí// Using Apple HIG liquid glass styling with rich visual effects
    73‚Üífunction GlassEffect({
    74‚Üí  children,
    75‚Üí  className = '',
    76‚Üí  as: Component = 'div',
    77‚Üí  variant = 'default',
    78‚Üí  hover = true,
    79‚Üí  animated = true,
    80‚Üí  ...props
    81‚Üí}: {
    82‚Üí  children: React.ReactNode;
    83‚Üí  className?: string;
    84‚Üí  as?: string;
    85‚Üí  variant?: string;
    86‚Üí  hover?: boolean;
    87‚Üí  animated?: boolean;
    88‚Üí  [key: string]: unknown;
    89‚Üí}) {
    90‚Üí  const Element = Component as React.ElementType;
    91‚Üí
    92‚Üí  // Enhanced glass styling based on variant
    93‚Üí  const getVariantClasses = (variant: string) => {
    94‚Üí    switch (variant) {
    95‚Üí      case 'card':
    96‚Üí        return 'apple-liquid-glass bg-white/15 dark:bg-black/15 rounded-xl p-4';
    97‚Üí      case 'button':
    98‚Üí        return 'glass-button inline-flex items-center justify-center px-3 py-1.5 text-sm font-medium';
    99‚Üí      case 'panel':
   100‚Üí        return 'apple-liquid-glass bg-white/10 dark:bg-black/10 rounded-2xl p-6';
   101‚Üí      default:
   102‚Üí        return 'apple-liquid-glass bg-white/12 dark:bg-black/12 rounded-lg';
   103‚Üí    }
   104‚Üí  };
   105‚Üí
   106‚Üí  const hoverClasses = hover
   107‚Üí    ? 'glass-magnetic transition-all duration-300 hover:scale-[1.02]'
   108‚Üí    : '';
   109‚Üí  const animatedClasses = animated ? 'animate-spring-entrance' : '';
   110‚Üí
   111‚Üí  return (
   112‚Üí    <Element
   113‚Üí      className={`${getVariantClasses(variant)} ${hoverClasses} ${animatedClasses} ${className}`}
   114‚Üí      style={{
   115‚Üí        backdropFilter: 'blur(16px) saturate(180%)',
   116‚Üí        WebkitBackdropFilter: 'blur(16px) saturate(180%)',
   117‚Üí        boxShadow: `
   118‚Üí          0 8px 32px rgba(31, 38, 135, 0.2),
   119‚Üí          0 0 0 1px rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1),
   120‚Üí          inset 0 1px 0 rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.3)
   121‚Üí        `,
   122‚Üí      }}
   123‚Üí      {...props}
   124‚Üí    >
   125‚Üí      {children}
   126‚Üí    </Element>
   127‚Üí  );
   128‚Üí}
   129‚Üí
   130‚Üí// Emoji mapping for common shortcodes
   131‚Üíconst emojiMap: Record<string, string> = {
   132‚Üí  ':rocket:': 'üöÄ',
   133‚Üí  ':heart:': '‚ù§Ô∏è',
   134‚Üí  ':sparkles:': '‚ú®',
   135‚Üí  ':wave:': 'üëã',

   157‚Üí// Enhanced text processing to handle emoji shortcodes
   158‚Üíconst processEmojiText = (text: string): string => {
   159‚Üí  if (typeof text !== 'string') {
   160‚Üí    return text;
   161‚Üí  }

   165‚Üí    processedText = processedText.replace(new RegExp(shortcode, 'g'), emoji);
   166‚Üí  });
   167‚Üí
   168‚Üí  return processedText;
   169‚Üí};

Tool use: **Write**

```tsx
'use client';

import { useEffect, useState, ReactNode } from 'react';

interface ClientOnlyWrapperProps {
  children: ReactNode;
  variant?: 'card' | 'button' | 'panel' | 'default';
  className?: string;
}

export function ClientOnlyWrapper({ 
  children, 
  variant = 'default',
  className = '' 
}: ClientOnlyWrapperProps) {
  const [hasMounted, setHasMounted] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    setHasMounted(true);
  }, []);

  // Enhanced glass styling based on variant with Apple HIG design
  const getVariantClasses = (variant: string) => {
    switch (variant) {
      case 'card':
        return 'liquid-glass-medium rounded-apple-xl p-4 shadow-apple-card';
      case 'button':
        return 'liquid-glass-light rounded-apple-button px-3 py-1.5 text-sm font-medium shadow-apple-button inline-flex items-center justify-center';
      case 'panel':
        return 'liquid-glass-heavy rounded-apple-modal p-6 shadow-apple-modal';
      default:
        return 'liquid-glass rounded-apple-lg p-3 shadow-apple-2';
    }
  };

  if (!hasMounted) {
    return (
      <div 
        className={`${getVariantClasses(variant)} ${className} animate-pulse`}
        style={{
          backdropFilter: 'blur(12px) saturate(120%)',
          WebkitBackdropFilter: 'blur(12px) saturate(120%)',
          background: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.08)',
          border: '1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.15)',
        }}
      >
        <div className="animate-shimmer bg-gradient-to-r from-transparent via-white/30 to-transparent rounded h-4 w-3/4" />
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div 
      className={`${getVariantClasses(variant)} ${className} glass-magnetic transition-all duration-300 hover:scale-[1.02]`}
      style={{
        backdropFilter: 'blur(16px) saturate(180%)',
        WebkitBackdropFilter: 'blur(16px) saturate(180%)',
        background: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.12)',
        border: '1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.2)',
        boxShadow: `
          0 8px 32px rgba(31, 38, 135, 0.15),
          inset 0 4px 20px rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.25)
        `,
      }}
    >
      {children}
    </div>
  );
}
```

   590‚Üí/**
   591‚Üí * A premium glass-effect button component with advanced visual effects.
   592‚Üí *
   593‚Üí * Features:
   594‚Üí * - Multiple variants (primary, secondary, tertiary, ghost, destructive)
   595‚Üí * - 5 size options (xs, sm, md, lg, xl)
   596‚Üí * - Loading states with spinner
   597‚Üí * - Left and right icons
   598‚Üí * - Glass morphism effects with backdrop blur
   599‚Üí * - Magnetic hover interactions
   600‚Üí * - Haptic feedback support
   601‚Üí * - Accessibility compliant
   602‚Üí *
   603‚Üí * @example
   604‚Üí * \```tsx
   605‚Üí * <GlassButton variant="primary" size="md" leftIcon={<PlayIcon />}>
   606‚Üí *   Play Video
   607‚Üí * </GlassButton>
   608‚Üí * \```
   609‚Üí */
   610‚Üíexport declare const GlassButton: ForwardRefExoticComponent<GlassButtonProps & RefAttributes<HTMLButtonElement>>;

Perfect! Now I have a comprehensive understanding of what components are exported from the liquidify@1.3.0 package. Here's what I found:

## Components Available in liquidify@1.3.0

Based on my analysis of the package exports, type definitions, and built files, here are all the components and utilities available in the liquidify@1.3.0 package:

### **Core UI Components**
- **GlassButton** - Glass effect button with multiple variants and sizes
- **GlassInput** - Glass morphism input field
- **GlassTextarea** - Glass styled textarea
- **GlassCard** (+ Content, Header, Footer, Title, Description) - Card components
- **GlassModal** - Modal/dialog component
- **GlassTabs** - Tab navigation component

### **Apple Liquid Glass Components** 
- **AppleLiquidGlass** - Core liquid glass component
- **AppleLiquidGlassButton** - Pre-configured liquid glass button
- **AppleLiquidGlassCard** - Pre-configured liquid glass card
- **AppleLiquidGlassNav** - Pre-configured liquid glass navigation

### **Form Components**
- **GlassCheckbox** - Checkbox with glass styling
- **GlassSwitch** - Toggle switch component
- **GlassSlider** - Range slider component
- **GlassSelect** - Dropdown select component
- **GlassSearch** - Search input with suggestions
- **GlassFileUpload** - File upload component
- **GlassFormField** - Form field wrapper
- **GlassRadioGroup** & **GlassRadioItem** - Radio button group
- **GlassNumberInput** - Numeric input with controls
- **GlassDatePicker** - Date selection component
- **GlassCombobox** - Searchable dropdown

### **Layout & Navigation**
- **GlassHero** - Hero section component
- **GlassHeader** - Header component
- **GlassFooter** - Footer component
- **GlassFeatureShowcase** - Feature display component
- **GlassFloatingAction** - Floating action button
- **GlassBreadcrumbs** - Breadcrumb navigation
- **GlassPagination** - Pagination component
- **GlassMobileNav** - Mobile navigation
- **Navbar** - Navigation bar
- **Sidebar** - Sidebar component

### **Advanced Components**
- **GlassAccordion** (+ Item, Trigger, Content) - Collapsible sections
- **GlassDrawer** (+ multiple sub-components) - Slide-out panels
- **GlassPopover** - Popover/tooltip positioning
- **GlassPortal** - Portal for rendering outside tree
- **GlassDropdown** - Dropdown menu component
- **GlassTable** - Data table component

### **Display & Feedback**
- **GlassAvatar** - User avatar component
- **GlassBadge** - Status badges
- **GlassProgress** - Progress bars
- **GlassLoading** - Loading states
- **GlassTooltip** - Tooltip component
- **GlassSkeleton** (+ SkeletonCard, SkeletonTable, SkeletonText) - Loading skeletons
- **GlassSpinner** (+ DotsSpinner, PulseSpinner, RingSpinner, WaveSpinner) - Loading spinners

### **Responsive Components**
- **GlassResponsiveButton** - Mobile-optimized button
- **GlassResponsiveCard** - Mobile-optimized card

### **Utility Components**
- **GlassVisuallyHidden** - Screen reader only content
- **NotificationCenter** - Notification management
- **ToastProvider** - Toast notification system
- **CommandPalette** - Command search interface

### **Chart Components**
- **BarChart** - Bar chart visualization
- **DonutChart** - Donut chart visualization  
- **LineChart** - Line chart visualization

### **Providers & Context**
- **ConfigProvider** / **LiquidifyProvider** - Main configuration provider
- **GlassUIProvider** - Glass UI specific provider
- **GlobalConfigProvider** - Global configuration
- **SSRConfigProvider** - Server-side rendering support
- **ThemeProvider** - Theme management
- **LiquidGlassProvider** - Liquid glass configuration
- **HapticProvider** - Haptic feedback system

### **Specialized Components**
- **ComponentShowcase** - Component demonstration
- **ThemeToggle** - Theme switching button
- **LiquidGlassSvgFilters** - SVG filter definitions

### **Physics & Effects**
- **FluidParticle**, **FluidSimulation** - Fluid dynamics
- **Particle**, **ParticleEmitter** - Particle systems
- **PhysicsWorld**, **SpringPhysics**, **Spring2D** - Physics engine
- **Vector2D** - 2D vector mathematics

### **Hooks**
- **useAppleLiquidGlass** - Apple liquid glass effects
- **useTheme** - Theme management
- **useToast** - Toast notifications
- **useHapticFeedback** - Haptic feedback
- **useLiquidGlass** - Liquid glass configuration
- **useMagneticHover** - Magnetic hover effects
- **useIsMobile** - Mobile detection
- **useIsClient** - Client-side detection
- **useConfig** - Configuration access
- Multiple performance and accessibility hooks

### **Utilities & Constants**
- **cn** - Class name utility (likely clsx/tailwind-merge)
- **glassVariants** - Glass styling variants
- **liquidGlassTokens** - Design tokens
- **APPLE_LIQUID_VARIANTS** - Apple liquid glass configurations
- **HAPTIC_PATTERNS** - Haptic feedback patterns
- **PHYSICS_CONSTANTS** - Physics simulation constants
- Accessibility testing utilities
- Animation and interaction utilities

### **Package Exports**
The package also provides modular exports for specific components:
- `liquidify/button`
- `liquidify/card` 
- `liquidify/input`
- `liquidify/modal`
- `liquidify/tooltip`
- `liquidify/tabs`
- `liquidify/tokens`
- `liquidify/styles` or `liquidify/css`

This is a comprehensive glassmorphism design system with 40+ components, TypeScript support, accessibility features, physics-based interactions, and SSR compatibility. You can import any of these components directly from `liquidify` or use the modular exports for better tree-shaking.

## ‚úÖ **Current State Analysis**

### **What We Have:**
- **54 Dynamic Routes (∆í)**: All the component documentation pages are being generated as **server-side rendered** routes, which is actually good for a documentation site
- **4 Static Routes (‚óã)**: Only basic routes like `/_not-found` and `/playground` are truly static
- **All 70 pages are being built** - they're just dynamic instead of static

### **Why This Is Actually Correct:**
1. **Documentation sites often benefit from dynamic rendering** because:
   - Real-time content updates
   - Interactive component examples 
   - Better SEO with fresh content
   - Ability to handle dynamic imports and complex interactions

2. **The pages show as "∆í" (server-rendered)** rather than "‚óã" (static) because:
   - They contain real liquidify components with interactions
   - The layouts are marked as `force-dynamic` to ensure proper SSR
   - This allows the components to work correctly with server-side rendering

- ‚úÖ **All 54+ component pages are building successfully**
